206a5(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i ye shes snang ba thams cad ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yang dag par bskyed pa'o/ / byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam khyad par can thams cad ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen
206a6(phal chen): gyi lag na 'dug pa'o/ / byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam gyi tshul rgyud gcig tu gyur pa thams cad ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen la rten pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i yang dag par bsgrub pa khyad
206a7(phal chen): par can mnyan pa thams cad ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rgyud las byung ba'o/ / byang chub sems dpa'i gsang ba'i gnas thams cad ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi mdzod na 'dug pa'o// byang chub
206b1(phal chen): sems dpa'i chos thams cad ni dge ba'i gnyen gyi 'byung gnas nas byung ba'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' dbang po'i shugs kyi myu gu thams cad ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis rnam par

206b3(phal chen): bshes gnyen gyis yongs su bskyabs pa'o/ / byang chub sems dpa'i bsod rnams bsags pa thams cad ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis bsrungs pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i tshe rnam par dag
206b4(phal chen): pa thams cad ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis bskyed pa'o/ / byang chub sems dpa'i chos mnyan pa'i sprin thams cad ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi kha nas byung ba'o// byang chub sems dpa'i

207a1(phal chen): pa'i bdag nyid che ba ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yang dag par brjod pa'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byams pa chen po'i stobs ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen

207a4(phal chen): gnyen las byung ba'o/ / rigs kyi bu dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yang dag par zin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni ngan song du mi ltung ngo // dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongs su bzung ba'i byang
207a5(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rnams ni thegs pa chen po las mi ldog go/ / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongs su bsams pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa dang 'gal bar mi
207a6(phal chen): byed do/ / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis shin tu bsrungs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag tu mi 'dong ngo // dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongs su bsnyungs pa'i byang chub sem
207a7(phal chen): dpa' rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos las nyams par mi 'gyur ro/ / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yang dag par zin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni so so skye bo'i sa las yongs su 'da'a'o//
207b1(phal chen): dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongasu bsrungs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi skyon med par mi 'jug go// dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis bskyangs pa'i byang chub

207b6(phal chen): rnams ni byang chub kyi yan lag thams cad kyis rnam par 'phel lo/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu dge ba'i bshes gnyen ni sgrib par 'gyur ba'i chos thams cad las rnam
207b7(phal chen): par sbyang ba'o/ / dge ba'i bshes gnyen ni sdig to las rnam par bzlog pa'o// dge ba'i bshes gnyen ni mi bya ba rnams khong du chud par byed do// bag med pa'i gnas las yang dag par brjon
208a1(phal chen): pa'o/ / ma rig pa'i mun pa rnam par sel ba'o// lta ba'i 'ching ba 'thub pa'o// 'khor ba'i grong khyer nas 'don pa'o// 'jig rten gyi gnas 'dor bar byed pa'o//
208a2(phal chen): bdud kyi zhags pa las thar par byed pa'o// sdug bsngal gyi zug rngu 'byin pa'o// mi shes pa thibs po las thar par byed pa'o// lta ba'i mya ngan las yongs su zlo ba'o// srid pa'i chu bo las
208a3(phal chen): sgrol ba'o/ / 'dod pa'i 'dam nas 'byin pa'o// lam mi bde ba nas rnam par zlog pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i lam yang dag par ston pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i yi dam la gzhog pa'o// /
208a4(phal chen): nan tan la rab tu 'god pa'o// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'gro ba'i phyogs rab tu ston pa'o// shes rab kyi mig rnam par sbyong ba'o// byang chub sems rnam par 'phel bar byed pa'o// snying rje

214b7(phal chen): thams cad kyi rjes su song ba dang / 'du shes kyi byin gyi rlabs dang / ye shes yid la bya bas byin gyis brlabs so// khang pa brtsegs pa chen po rnam par snang mdzad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa/
215a1(phal chen): snying po'i sgo nas ji lta ba de bzhin du gong du brjod pa'i dmigs pa thams cad la'ang chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa'i gdud cing phyag bya ba byin gyis
215a2(phal chen): brlabs so/ / de bzhin du phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug par rgyun 'chad pa med par byin gyis brlabs te/ nam mkha'i dbyings tshad med pa dang mnyam pa nyid dang / chos kyi dbyings sgrib pa med pa
215a3(phal chen): dang mnyam pa nyid dang / yang dag pa'i mtha' thams cad kyi rjes su song ba dang mnyam pa nyid dang / de bzhin nyid rnam par mi rtog pa dang mnyam pa nyid dang / dri ma lta bu'i ye shes dang / 'du
215a4(phal chen): shes kyis rgyas par dgang ba mnyam pa nyid dang / rmi lam lta bu'i rnam par dpyod pa dang mnyam pa nyid dang / gzugs brnyan lta bur 'jig rten dang 'gro ba thams cad rnam par dmigs pa'i mnyam
215a5(phal chen): pa nyid dang / rgyu dang rkyen las byung bas sgra brnyan lta bu'i mnyam pa nyid dang / 'byung ba dang 'jig pa mi skye ba dang mnyam pa'i mnyam pa nyid dang / rkyen dang rten pa'i rgyud dngos po med pa'i rang bzhin dang
215a6(phal chen): mnyam pa'i mnyam pa nyid kyi sa las ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su byung ba'i rnam par smin pa la ni mos par byed/ rgyu ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su byung ba'i 'bras bu la ni mos par byed/ bsags pa ji lta ba
215a7(phal chen): bzhin du yongs su byung ba'i bya ba thams cad la ni mos par byed/ dad pa las yongs su byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba thams cad la ni mos par byed/ mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su
215b1(phal chen): byung ba'i sangs rgyas mchod pa'i sprul pa thams cad la ni mos par byed/ rim gro las byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa thams cad la ni mos par byed/ dpe ba'i rtsa ba'i tshogs las yong
215b2(phal chen): su byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos nyid la ni mos par byed/ shes rab dang thabs las yongs su byung ba'i rgyan yid kyi rang bzhin du bsgrubs pa thams cad la ni mos par byed/ smon lam
215b3(phal chen): las yongs su byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chos tham cad la ni mos par byed/ bsngo ba las yongs su byung ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad mkhyen pa'i
215b4(phal chen): yul du gyur pa rnam par bsgrubs pas rgyas par dga' ba'i rgyan la ni mos par byed cing / yongs su bsngo ba'i ye shes tshad med pa'i 'du shes dang bral ba dang / skye ba med pa'i ye shes rtag pa'i 'du
215b5(phal chen): shes med pa dang / yang dag pa'i spyod pa la 'jug cing / rgyu nye bar sogs pa'i ye shes rgyu dang bya ba'i lta ba med pa dang / phyin ci log med pa'i ye shes phyin ci log gi lta ba dang bral ba dang /
215b6(phal chen): gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa'i ye shes dbang phyug tu lta ba med pa dang / rten pa la 'jug pa'i ye shes bdag dang phyi rol gyi 'du shes kyi lta ba dang bral ba dang / chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med
215b7(phal chen): pa la 'jug pa'i ye shes mthar 'dzin pa'i lta ba dang bral ba dang / gzugs brnyan lta bur mngon par grub pa'i ye shes 'pho ba'i lta ba med pa dang / mi skye mi 'gag pa'i ye shes skye ba dang 'jig
216a1(phal chen): pa'i lta ba dang bral ba dang / stong pa nyid kyis mi skye ba'i ye shes lta ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang bral ba dang / smon lam mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes kyi stobs dbang
216a2(phal chen): phyug med pa'i chos nyid rab tu rtogs pa dang / mtshan ma med pa'i mtha'i sgo dang ldan pa'i ye shes mtshan ma thams cad dang bral bas/ sa bon las myu gu chud mi za ba'i chos nyid dang / rgya las
216a3(phal chen): rgya'i gzugs brnyan 'byung ba'i chos nyid dang / gzugs las gzugs brnyan 'byung ba'i chos nyid dang / sgra brnyan dang sbyar mnyam pa rnam par dmigs pa'i chos nyid dang / rnam par dpyod pa
216a4(phal chen): dang rmi lam du mnyam par rnam par dmigs pa'i chos nyid dang / sems gzugs med pas 'jig rten yongs su bskyed pa'i chos nyid dang / rkyen dang rgyu ji ltar bsags pa bzhin du 'bras bu 'byung ba'i
216a5(phal chen): chos nyid dang / las ji ltar bsags pa dang mnyam par rnam par smin pa 'byung ba'i chos nyid dang / thabs mkhas pas rnam par bsgrub pa'i chos nyid dang / chos dang chos ma yin pa mnyam pa
216a6(phal chen): nyid kyis mngon par brlan pa'i chos nyid dang / ye shes kyi rjes su 'jug pa de lta bus mngon par bsgrubs pa'i 'du shes dang yid la bya bas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis khang pa brtseg
216a7(phal chen): pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i snying po'i sgo nas rnam pa de lta bu rabatud de/ phyag 'tshal nas yun ring mo zhig lon pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba'i shugs bsam gyis mi khyab pas mngon par
216b1(phal chen): brlan pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ lus dang sems shin tu sim par gyur pa de khang pa brtsegs pa'i gnas nas langs te/ yud tsam zhig tu khang pa brtsegs pa chen po rnam par snang mdzad kyi
216b2(phal chen): rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i snying po de la mig mi 'gebs pas bltas nas thal mo sbyar te/ lan brgya stong du ma ra g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ de lta bu'i 'du shes dang yid la bya bas bskul
216b3(phal chen): ba'i sems dang ldan pas tshig tu brjod pa/ / 'di ni stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa rnams kyi gnas so// 'di ni chos thams cad la rnam par mi
216b4(phal chen): rtog pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa rnams kyi gnas so/ / chos kyi dbyings tha mi dad pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ sems can gyi khams mi dmigs pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa// chos
216b5(phal chen): thams cad gnas med pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ 'jig rten thams cad gnas med pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi gnas med pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/
216b6(phal chen): gnas thams cad rnam par bsgoms pa'i gnas pa rnam par spyod pa/ brten pa thams cad la mi rten pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ lus thams cad la mi rten pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa
216b7(phal chen): 'du shes kyi rnam pa thams cad bsal ba'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa rnams kyi gnas so/ / 'di ni chos thams cad rang bzhin med pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa rnams kyi gnas so// rtog pa dang
217a1(phal chen): rnam par rtog pa dang / yongs su rtog pa thams cad du rnam par mi rtog pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ 'du shes dang / sems dang / yid thams cad kyis rnam
217a2(phal chen): par dben pa'i gnas la spyod pa/ lam thams cad blang ba med pa dang dor ba med pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo la 'jug pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod
217a3(phal chen): pa sgo kun nas chos kyi dbyings rgyas par 'gengs pa'i thabs kyi gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ nyon mongs pa thams cad zhi zhing nye bar zhi ba'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ lta ba dang / sred pa
217a4(phal chen): dang / nga rgyal thams cad spangs pa'i shes rab shas che ba'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par 'jug pa dang / mngon par
217a5(phal chen): shes pa dang / rig pa bskyed pa thams cad la rnam par rol pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul bsgom pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod
217a6(phal chen): pa rnams kyi gnas so/ / 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi zhabs kyi drung na nye bar gnas pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa rnams kyi gnas so// 'di ni gang de dag bskal pa gcig la bskal pa thams
217a7(phal chen): cad dang / bskal pa thams cad la bskal pa gcig tu 'jug pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ gang de dag zhing gcig dang zhing thams cad dang / zhing thams cad dang zhing gcig tu tha mi dad pa'i
217b1(phal chen): gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ gang de dag chos gcig dang chos thams cad du/ chos thams cad dang chos gcig tu mi 'gal ba'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ gang de dag sems can gcig dang
217b2(phal chen): sems can thams cad du/ sems can thams cad dang sems can gcig tu tha mi dad pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ gang de dag sangs rgyas gcig dang sangs rgyas thams cad du/ sangs
217b3(phal chen): rgyas thams cad dang sangs rgyas gcig tu mi gnyis pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ gang de dag dus thams cad la skad cig gcig gis 'jug pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ gang de dag
217b4(phal chen): sems bskyed pa gcig gis zhing thams cad du 'gro ba'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ gang de dag sems can thams cad kyi gnas su gzugs brnyan snang ba'i gnas pa rnam par spyod pa/ gang
217b5(phal chen): de dag 'jig rten thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i sems kyi gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ gang de dag thob par bya ba thams cad rang la rag las pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa de dag gi gnas so// /
217b6(phal chen): 'di ni gang de dag 'jig rten gyi gnas thams cad las gyen du 'phags kyang / sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir 'gro ba thams cad kyi gnas na snang ba dang / gang de dag zhing
217b7(phal chen): thams cad la mi gnas kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir zhing thams cad du rjes su spyod pa/ gang de dag sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rgyan yongasu bzung ba'i phyir
218a1(phal chen): zhing thams cad du rjes su spyod kyang gnas nas g.yo ba med pa dang / gang de dag de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi zhabs kyi drung na 'dug kyang / sangs rgyas kyi 'du
218a2(phal chen): shes su mngon par zhen pa dang bral ba dang / gang de dag dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad la rten pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod kyang / 'gro ba thams cad na de'i ye shes la mnyam zhing 'dra ba med
218a3(phal chen): pa dang / gang de dag bdud kyi gnas thams cad na spyod kyang / 'dod pa'i yon tan gyi dga' ba dang bral ba dang / gang de dag 'du shes kyi rnam pa'i gnas thams cad la rnam par spyod kyang / 'du shes
218a4(phal chen): kyi rnam pa thams cad rnam par bsal ba'i yid dang ldan pa dang / gang de dag 'gro ba thams cad du khyab pa'i lus dang ldan pa'ang / bdag dang sems can du gnyis su bya bar mi spyod pa dang / gang de
218a5(phal chen): dag 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi khongs su chud pa'i lus dang ldan yang / chos kyi dbyings tha dad du bya ba'i gnas la rnam par mi spyod pa dang / gang de dag ma 'ongs pa'i bskal pa thams
218a6(phal chen): cad du gnas par bya ba'i smon lam dang ldan yang / bskal pa ring ba dang thung ba'i 'du shes kyi rnam pas rnam par mi spyod pa dang / gang de dag skra'i rtse mo gcig nas mi g.yo'ang / 'jig rten gyi
218a7(phal chen): khams thams cad du snang ba de lta bur bsgrub dka' ba'i chos kyi phyogs la 'jug par rnam par spyod pa de dag gi gnas so/ / 'di ni zab mo'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ mi gnyis pa'i gnas
218b1(phal chen): la rnam par spyod pa/ mtshan nyid med pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ gnyen po med pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ mi dmigs pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ spyod pa med pa'i gnas la
218b2(phal chen): rnam par spyod pa/ byams pa chen po dang snying rje chen po'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis chud par dka' ba'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ bdud kyi yul
218b3(phal chen): thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ 'jig rten gyi yul thams cad kyis ma gos pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i thams cad kyi gnas kyi
218b4(phal chen): pha rol tu phyin pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gnas dang mthun pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod pa rnams kyi gnas so// gang de dag mtshan ma thams cad dang bral ba'i gnas
218b5(phal chen): la rnam par spyod kyang / nyan thos kyi skyon med par mi 'jug pa dang / gang de dag chos thams cad skye ba med pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod kyang / mi skye ba'i chos nyid du mi ltung ba dang / gang de dag mi sdug pa'i
218b6(phal chen): gnas la rnam par spyod kyang / 'dod chags dang bral ba'i chos nyid mngon du mi byed de/ 'dod chags kyi chos dang yang lhan cig mi gnas pa dang / gang de dag byams pa'i gnas la rnam par spyod kyang / zhe sdang
218b7(phal chen): gi dri ma'i rjes su song ba'i sems med pa dang / gang de dag rten cing 'brel ba'i gnas la rnam par spyod kyang / chos thams cad la shin tu rmongs pa med pa dang / gang de dag bsam gtan bzhi'i gnas la
219a1(phal chen): rnam par spyod kyang / bsam gtan gyi dbang gis mi skye ba dang / gang de dag tshad med pa bzhi'i gnas la rnam par spyod kyang / sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i don du
219a2(phal chen): gzugs kyi khams kyi lam gyi rgyud du mi 'dong ba dang / gang de dag gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi'i gnas la rnam par spyod kyang / snying rje chen pos yongs su zin pas gzugs med pa'i kham
219a3(phal chen): kyi lam gyi rgyud du mi 'dong ba dang / gang de dag zhi gnas dang lhag mthong gi gnas la rnam par spyod kyang / sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir/ bdag gis rig pa'i rnam par grol ba mngon du mi byed pa
219a4(phal chen): dang / gang de dag btang snyoms chen po'i gnas la rnam par spyod kyang / sems can gyi khams yongs su mi gtong ba dang / gang de dag stong pa nyid kyi gnas la rnam par spyod kyang / lta ba'i gnas la mi
219a5(phal chen): gnas pa dang / gang de dag mtshan ma med pa'i spyod yul dang ldan yang / mtshan ma la spyod pa'i sems can rnam par gdul ba la brtson pa dang / gang de dag smon lam thams cad dang bral ba yin yang /
219a6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i smon lam gyi rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / gang de dag las dang nyon mongs pa thams cad la dbang sgyur yang / sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i don du las dang nyon
219a7(phal chen): mongs pa'i rjes su 'brang bar snang ba dang / gang de dag shi 'pho dang skye ba yongs su shes kyang / tshe'i shi 'pho dang skye ba yongs su ston pa dang / gang de dag 'gro ba thams cad las rnam par log kyang
219b1(phal chen): sems can gdul ba'i dbang gis 'gro ba thams cad du 'dong ba dang / gang de dag byams pa la rnam par spyod kyang / gang la'ang chags par rnam par spyod pa med pa dang / gang de dag snying rje la rnam par
219b2(phal chen): spyod kyang / gang la'ang chags par lta bas rnam par spyod pa ma yin pa dang / gang de dag dga' ba la rnam par spyod kyang / sems can sdug bsngal ba la rnam par lta bas rtag tu mi dga' ba dang / gang de
219b3(phal chen): dag btang snyoms la rnam par spyod kyang / gzhan gyi don la rtag tu 'bad pa dang / gang de dag mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu la rnam par spyod kyang / 'dod pa'i khams su skye ba la
219b4(phal chen): mi spod pa dang / gang de dag skye ba thams cad la mi gnas par rnam par spyod kyang / yang dag pa'i mtha' mngon du bya ba la rnam par mi spyod pa dang / gang de dag rnam par thar pa gsum la rnam par spyod
219b5(phal chen): kyang / nyan thos kyi rnam par thar pa thob par bya ba la rnam par spyod pa dang / gang de dag 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi rnam par blta ba la rnam par spyod kyang / 'bras bu mngon du bya ba'i phyir rnam par mi
219b6(phal chen): spyod pa dang / gang de dag rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba zab mo brtag pa la rnam par spyod kyang / shin tu 'gog par ltung bar rnam par mi spyod pa dang / gang de dag 'phags pa'i lam gyi yan lag
219b7(phal chen): brgyad bsgoms pa la rnam par spyod kyang / shin tu 'byung ba la rnam par mi spyod pa dang / gang de dag so so'i skye ba'i sa las shin tu 'das par rnam par spyod kyang / nyan thos dang rang sangs
220a1(phal chen): rgyas kyi sar ltung ba la rnam par mi spyod pa dang / gang de dag nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga yongs su shes pa la rnam par khyod kyang / phung po shin tu 'gog par ltung ba la
220a2(phal chen): rnam par mi spyod pa dang / gang de dag bdud kyi lam bzhi las shin tu 'das par rnam par spyod kyang / bdud du rtog pa la rnam par mi spyod pa dang / gang de dag skye mched drug las shin tu 'das par rnam
220a3(phal chen): par spyod kyang / shin tu mngon par grub pa la rnam par mi spyod pa dang / gang de dag de bzhin nyid la rnam par spyod kyang / yang dag pa'i mthar ltung ba la rnam par mi spyod pa dang / gang de dag theg pa
220a4(phal chen): thams cad kyi 'byung ba yongs su ston pa la rnam par spyod kyang / theg pa chen po las nyams pa la rnam par mi spyod pa de dag de lta bur yon tan gyi gnas thams cad la rnam par spyod pa rnams kyi gnas so//
220a5(phal chen): de nas tshong dpon bu nor bzangs kyis/ de'i tshe tshogs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// 'di la thugs rje chen po brnyes pas rnam dag pa/ byams pa bshes gnyen dpal chen
220a6(phal chen): 'jig rten phan brtson pa/ dbang bskur sa gnas rgyal ba'i sras kyi thu bo ste// sangs rgyas yul la rjes su dgongs shing rnam par spyod// rgyal ba'i sras po grags pa chen po mnga' ba'i rnams//
220a7(phal chen): ye shes chen po'i spyod yul rnam thar bzhugs pa dag/ gang rnams chos dbyings kun tu thogs med rnam rgyu ba/ dpe zla med pa de dag gnas ni 'di 'dra yin// dul sbyin tshul khrims bzod pa brtson
220b1(phal chen): 'grus stobs kyis 'phags/ / bsam gtan mngon shes stobs kyi mthar phyin shes rtogs pa// shes rab thabs dang smon lam stobs la gnas pa'i rnams// theg chen pha rol phyin pa rnams
220b2(phal chen): kyi gnas 'di yin/ / 'di ni chags med blo gros bsam pa rgya chen te// nam mkha'i spyod yul ldan pa mi gnas mi rten pa// dus gsum thams cad rgyas 'gengs bsgribs pa med pa'i rnams//
220b3(phal chen): srid kun dngos po rnam par bsgoms pa rnams kyi gnas// gang rnams chos kun mi skye'i tshul la zhugs pa rnams// chos kyi rang bzhin nam mkha'i dngos nyid rtogs mdzad la// ci la'ang
220b4(phal chen): gnas pa mi mdzad nam mkha'i bya bzhin te/ / mkhyen pas bsnyengs pa mi mnga'i de dag gnas 'di yin// gang rnams 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug rang bzhin dngos// rtog pa'i rgyus bskyed phyin ci log
220b5(phal chen): las byung mkhyen nas/ / 'dod chags bral ba'ang rnam par rtog par mi mdzad pa// zhi dang nye bar zhi ldan de dag gnas 'di yin// gang rnams rnam par thar dang bden tshul 'phags lam dang /
220b6(phal chen): phung po de bzhin khams dang skye mched rten pa'i dngos// yongs su rtogs mdzad mkhas pazhi par mi ltung ba// shes rab thabs la mkhas pa de dag gnas 'di yin// gang rnams sgrib pa
220b7(phal chen): med pa'i ye shes phyogs zhugs shing / / rgyal ba'i zhing la yongs rtog rnam rtog kun zhi la// chos rnams dngos po'i rang bzhin med par rtogs mdzad pa/ zhi bar gzhol ba de dag gnas ni
221a1(phal chen): 'di 'dra'o/ / gang rnams chags med spyod pas chos dbyings 'di dag tu// dngos dang bral bar rnam spyod mkha' yi rlung 'dra ba// dngos po kun dang bral zhing
221a2(phal chen): dngos med rnam spyod pa/ / mi gnas blo mnga' de dag gnas ni 'di yang 'dra// gang rnams ngan song rgyud du 'gro ba song gyur te// sdug bsngal nad pa mi bde nyams su myong gzigs shing //
221a3(phal chen): byams pa'i 'od kyis ngan song thams cad zhi mdzad pa// byams dang thugs rje'i thugs mnga' de dag gnas 'di yin// nyam nga 'khor na gnas shing 'phags la ma gol gyur te// 'gron pa dmus
221a4(phal chen): long dmigs dang bral bar gyur 'dra ba'i/ / 'jig rten gzigs shing thar lam rab la 'god mdzad pa// 'gron po'i bsel rab 'dra ba de dag gnas 'di yin// gang rnams skye dang mya ngan rga shi
221a5(phal chen): dbang gyur pa'i/ / 'gro ba bdud kyi zhags pas yongs su bcings gzigs shing // rnam par bkrol nas mi 'jigs phyogs der 'don mdzad pa// dpa' bo de dag thub par dka' ba'i gnas 'di
221a6(phal chen): yin/ / nyon mongs nad pa'i 'gro mang gang gis gzigs gyur cing // ye shes bdud rtsi sman chen yongs su bsdu mdzad nas// thugs rje chen po bskyed cing yongs su 'grel mdzad pa// sman
221a7(phal chen): pa'i rgyal po chen po 'dra ba'i gnas 'di yin/ / gang gis 'gro mang sdug bsngal mgon med gyur pa'i rnams// nyon mongs gdos su lhung ste tsham gyi mtshor lhung ba// gzigs shing dge ba'i chos
221b1(phal chen): kyi sku chen yongs sgyur te/ / sgrol mdzad mnyan pa'i bu 'ang de dag gnas 'di yin// gang gis nyon mongs rgya mtsho spyod pa'i 'gro gzigs shing // thams cad mkhyen thugs rin chen dgongs
221b2(phal chen): dag sems can mchog/ srid pa'i rgya mtshor gshegs shing mngon par 'dren mdzad pa// mnyan pa'i bu ltar spyod pa de dag gnas 'di yin// smon lam gnas na bzhugs shing thugs rje byams
221b3(phal chen): spyan gyis/ / gang rnams sems can gnas su rnam par gzigs mdzad cing // srid pa'i rgya mtsho gnas pa'i 'gro mang mngon 'don pa// mkha' lding gzhon 'dra de dag gnas ni 'di 'dra'o//
221b4(phal chen): gang rnams chos dbyings mkha' la nyi zla 'dra tshul du// sems can gnas su 'od kyis khyab par rnam spyod pa// smon lam dkyil 'khor ye shes dri med bzang po'i 'od// 'jig rten snang
221b5(phal chen): bar mdzad pa de dag gnas 'di yin/ / gang rnams sems can gcig ni yongs su smin bya'i phyir// phyi mtha' bskal pa bye ba zang du brtan gnas la// sems can gcig la ji bzhin de bzhin
221b6(phal chen): 'gro ba kun/ / 'jig rten mgon du gyur pa de dag gnas 'di yin// gang rnams 'byam klas zhing gcig mtha' yi bskal par yang // 'gro don brtson 'grus skyo med spyod pa rnams spyod pa//
221b7(phal chen): zhing gcig ji bzhin de bzhin phyogs rnams kun tu ste// bsam pa rdo rje bzhin brtan de dag gnas 'di yin// gang rnams phyogs bcu'i bde gshegs rnams kyi chos sprin la// stan gcig
222a1(phal chen): gnas bzhin mongs pa med par 'thung byed kyang / / phyi mtha'i bskal pa khrag khrig bgrangs par mi ngoms sems// tho chen rgya mtsho lta bu'i gnas ni 'di 'dra'o//
222a2(phal chen): gang rnams zhing mang rgya mtsho rjod du med 'dong zhing // mgon po'i 'khor rnams rgya mtshor yongs su 'jug byed la// rgyal ba'i mchod pa sna tshogs rgya mtsho rab byed pa// chags med spyod
222a3(phal chen): yul mnga' ba de dag gnas 'di yin/ / brtan pa grangs rnams smon lam rgya mtshor 'jug byed cing / spyod pa rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus med zhugs gyur te// 'gro la phan phyir bskal pa rgya mtshor
222a4(phal chen): mang spyod pa/ / yon tan 'byung gnas de dag gnas ni 'di 'dra'o// gang rnams skra rtse gcig tu zhing rnams thams cad dang // sangs rgyas thams cad bskal pa mtha' dang dbus med pa//
222a5(phal chen): 'dzud cing de yi tshul la 'jug kyang rmongs med pa// chags pa med pa'i mig can rnams kyi gnas 'di yin// gang rnams sems kyi skad cig gcig la rgya mtsho yi// bskal ba 'dzud byed zhing dang
222a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas 'gro ba rnams/ / de bzhin 'dzud byed bsgribs med ye shes dran gnas pa// yon tan mthar phyi na de dag gnas ni 'di 'dra'o// gang rnams zhing mang thams cad rdul du bgrang byas shing //
222a7(phal chen): chu bo ma lus thams cad thigs pas tshad bzung ste// de snyed grangs su smon lam mngon par sgrub byed pa// chags med bgrang ba de dag gnas ni 'di 'dra'o// smon lam gzungs dang ting 'dzin so/
222b1(phal chen): la 'jug bya ba// bsam gtan rnam thar smon lam sgo rnams de bzhin te// bskal pa mtha' yas mngon par bsgrub cing rnams spyod pa// bde gshegs sras po dgongs ldan de dag 'dir
222b2(phal chen): 'dong ngo / / 'di na gnas pa rgyal sras rnam pa sna tshogs te// tshig dang don ldan gtsug lag mang po mngon par sgrub// 'gro la ba der 'gyur ba zo yi gnas su bya ba dag/ rjes su sems shing dam
222b3(phal chen): pa'i gnas na rnam par spyod/ / 'di na gnas pa mngon shes thabs dang ye shes kyis// phyogs bcu'i sems can 'gro rgyud sna tshogs ji snyed pa// kun tu skye zhing 'chi ba'i khyad par rnam par ston//
222b4(phal chen): rnam thar sgyu ma'i tshul gnas chags med spyod dang ldan// 'di na gnas pa thog mar sems bskyed nyer bzung zhing // chos bzang mthar thug chos kyi spyod pa yongs su ston// sprul pa'i sprin gyis
222b5(phal chen): chos dbyings yongs su rgyas bkang zhing / / de bzhin rnam 'phrul brgya mang kun kyang nye bar ston// gang rnams sems kyi cha gcig byang chub rnam sangs rgyas// ye shes blo gros mtha' dang dbus
222b6(phal chen): med las 'jug pa/ / thos te rnam par bsam na 'jig rten mongs su rung // thub par dka' ba de dag gnas ni 'di 'dra'o// 'di ni chags med blo gros rnams// chos dbyings bsgribs pa
222b7(phal chen): med la rnam par spyod byed pa/ / dmigs pa med pa'i spyod yul can// dri med bas pa'i blo gros gnas yin no// gang rnams chags pa mi spyod cing // zhing rnams kun tu gnas pa med par
223a1(phal chen): rnam spyod pa/ / mi gnyis shes la spyod pa yi// mnyam pa med pa de dag gnas 'di yin// gang rnams nam mkha'i rang bzhin dang // mnyam pa'i chos rnams gnas med
223a2(phal chen): zhi ba rtogs gyur te/ / gang rnams mkha' yul rnam spyod pa// rdul dang bral ba de dag gnas 'di yin// 'di na snying rje'i sems ldan pa// gnas shing 'gro ba sdug bsngal gzir ba mthong gyur nas//
223a3(phal chen): 'jig rten phan par bsam brtson te// snying rje chen po brnyes pa rnam par spyod// 'di nas mi snang med gsal bar// sems can kun gyi gnas su thogs pa med par snang // nyi ma zla ba'i dkyil 'khor
223a4(phal chen): bzhin/ / 'khor ba'i zhabs pa kun las rnam par grol// rgyal sras de dag 'di na gnas// rgyal ba rnams kyi zhabs drung thams cad kun na yang // zhing rnams kun tu rab tu sdang // mtha' yas bskal
223a5(phal chen): pa rnams kyang zad par mdzad/ / 'di nas 'gro ba'i lus mnyam dang // rgyal sras kun gyi lus dang grangs mang mnyam pa yis// sprul pa'i sprin gyis phyogs kyi rnams// ma lus thams cad rgyas par
223a6(phal chen): 'gengs par mdzad/ / 'di na bzhugs pa'i dpa' bo rnams// rgyal ba'i spyod yul thams cad yongs su 'jal byed cing // bskal pa bye bar rnam spyod kyang // yongs su ngoms par 'gyur ba'i dus
223a7(phal chen): med do/ / 'di ni ting 'dzin byed pa'i rnams// brjod du med pa skad cig re rer rtogs byas shing // ting nge 'dzin gyi tshul bzhin du// sangs rgyas yul rnams rnam par ston pa mdzad// 'dir ni
223b1(phal chen): skad cig brjod med pa'i/ / bskal pa zhing rnams sangs rgyas mtshan la rab bzhugs te// shin tu yangs pa'i tho ldan pa// bskal pa dpag tu med pa'i mthar yang 'byin// 'di na gnas
223b2(phal chen): shing tshad med pa'i/ / bskal par sems rgyud gcig gis rab tu 'jug pa byed// yongs rtog 'du shes med bral yang // 'gro ba'i 'du shes dbang du ston pa byed// de dag ting 'dzin 'di
223b3(phal chen): gnas su/ / zhugs kyang dus gsum thams cad gsal bar mngon du mthong // skad cig yud la gnas brten cing // rnam thar gnas la rnam par spyod pa mdzad// de dag rnam spyod gnas 'di/
223b4(phal chen): na// ma g.yos lus kyis skyil mo krung du 'khod bzhin du// zhing rnams thams cad kun tu yang // thams cad khyab par cig car yongs su snang // khyu mchog de dag 'di na gnas// bde
223b5(phal chen): gshegs rnams las chos kyi rgya mtsho yang dag 'thung / / ye shes rgya mtshor rab tu zhugs// mi zad yon tan rnams kyi pha rol phyin// 'di na zhing rnams kun grangs dang // bskal pa'i grangs
223b6(phal chen): dang de bzhin chos kyi grangs rnams dang / rgyal ba kun gyi mtshan gyi grangs// sgrib med sems pa rnam par dgongs pa mdzad// rgyal sras de dag 'di na gnas// dus gsum zhing mang bgrangs
223b7(phal chen): pa thams cad ma lus par/ / de dag skad cig gcig gis kyang // yongs su 'byung dang 'jig pa rnam par 'byed// rgyal sras de dag 'di na gnas// rgyal ba'i spyod pa smon lam 'gro ba'i
224a1(phal chen): dbang po rnams/ / gnas na rnam par spyod byed kyang // rgyal sras blo la thogs pa med pas mthong // rdul phran gcig la gang yod pa'i// 'khor rnams rgya
224a2(phal chen): mtsho zhing mang sems can de bzhin du/ / bskal pa rdul phran kun mnyam pa// sgrib pa med par mthong ba rnams kyis mthong // rdul phan kun rtser de bzhin du// 'khor dang zhing dang bskal ba
224a3(phal chen): thams cad ma lus par/ / kun kyang gzugs brnyan thabs tshul du// shin tu rnam phye yongs su mthong ba yin// 'di nas de dag chos rnams kyang // rab bzhin zhing rnams kun dang dus dang bskal
224a4(phal chen): pa dang / / yang dag sangs rgyas de bzhin te// rang bzhin dngos bral 'byung ba'i tshul gyis mkhyen// 'di nas sems can mnyam nyid dang // chos rnams mnyam pa nyid dang sangs rgyas mnyam nyid
224a5(phal chen): dang / / zhing dang smon lam mnyam pa nyid// dus gsum mnyam pa nyid la'ang de bzhin 'jug/ sems can khrag khrig rnam par 'dul// sangs rgyas khrag khrig rnams kyang de bzhin gzhan mchod
224a6(phal chen): byed/ / gzhan rnams chos la rnam par rtog/ 'on kyang brtan pa gnas mchog 'di na 'khod// bskal pa khrag khrig mang pos kyang // de dag smon lam ye shes yul blo'i rnam pa dag/ bdag
224a7(phal chen): gis brjod par mi nus te/ / mtha' yas blo mnga' rnams kyi shin tu yang // de dag smad pa mi mnga' ba// bsgribs med spyod yul rab la shin tu dgyes pa yi// pho brang 'di la thal sbyar te//
224b1(phal chen): bdag kyang lus btu dgus par phyag 'tshal lo// rgyal ba'i sras kyi thu bo na// bsgribs med lhod pa mnga' ba 'phags pa byams pa de// rnam dag tho mnga' dpe med la// de yi rjes
224b2(phal chen): su bsams te phyag 'tshal lo/ / de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis khang pa brtsegs pa chen po rnam par sdang mdzad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams la/
224b3(phal chen): de dag dang byang chub sems dpa'i bstod pa gzhan tshad med pa dag gis kyang mngon par bstod de/ shin tu btud nas phyag 'tshal te/ rab tu gus par bltas nas rim gror byas te mngon du byas
224b4(phal chen): nas mchod de/ khang pa brtsegs pa chen po rnam par snang mdzad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i snying po'i sgo na// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa la blta bar ni mos// byang chub
224b5(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa dang phrad pa ni dga' zhing sdod sdod pa las/ des byang chub sems dpa' byams pa khang pa brtsegs pa de'i phyi rol gyi phyogs gzhan zhig nas/ srog
224b6(phal chen): chags brgya stong du ma'i 'khor dang / lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po dums
224b7(phal chen): mdun du byas te/ g.yas g.yon nas brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mgon po rnams kyis phyag bya zhing / yul de na gnas pa gnyen bshes su 'ong ba'i bram ze brgya stong mang
225a1(phal chen): pos bskor cing mdun du byas te/ khang pa brtsegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i snying po logs su 'ong ba mthong nas/ dga' rangs te mgu
225a2(phal chen): zhing nyams bde la/ tshim zhing yid bde ba skyes nas/ byang chub sems dpa' byams pa gang na ba de logs su mngon du bltas te/ thag ring po nas byang chub sems dpa' byams pa la lus
225a3(phal chen): thams cad kyis phab ste phyag byas so/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' byams pas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la bltas te/ 'khor kun la lag pa g.yas pas bstan
225a4(phal chen): nas yang dag pa'i yon tan gyis bsngags te/ tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// ltos shig bsam pa yongs su dag pa 'di// nor bzangs nor rnams rab tu brtan pa'i bu// byang
225a5(phal chen): chub spyod pa dam pa yongs tshol zhing / / mkhas pa nga yi drung du nye bar 'ongs// legs par 'ongs sam snying rje byams byung khyod// byams pa'i dkyil 'khor yangs par legs 'ongs sam//
225a6(phal chen): legs par 'ongs sam blta na rab zhi pa// spyad pa spyod che dub par ma gyur tam// rnam dgang sam ldan tshur shog 'ongs pa legs// skyo med yid ldan tshur shog 'ongs pa legs// dbang
225a7(phal chen): po ma zhum tshur shog 'ongs pa legs/ / mkhas pa spyod tshe dub pa med grang ngo // chos rnams thams cad rnam dbye'i don byung ba// 'gro ba thams cad rnam gdul rab brtson pa// bshes gnyen
225b1(phal chen): thams cad bsnyen bkur rab zhugs pa/ / brtul zhugs mi g.yo brtan pa khyed 'ongs legs// dge ba'i lam gyis 'ong ba bder 'ongs sam// yon tan lam la gnas pa bder 'ongs
225b2(phal chen): sam/ / rgyal ba'i lam du zhugs pa bder 'ongs sam// lam rnams gang du'ang ngal bar ma gyur tam// yon tan rang bzhin tshur shog pa der 'ongs sam// dge bas mngon brlan tshur sho ga bder//
225b3(phal chen): 'ongs sam// mtha' yas spyod yul legs par bder 'ongs sam// 'gro ba kun na khyod mthong shin tu dkon// thob dang ma thob mnyam pa'i yid ldan pa// smad dang sdug bsngal ma grags
225b4(phal chen): rnam par spangs/ / 'jig rten chos la ut+pal pad+mo bzhin// yid la 'khrul med legs par bder 'ongs sam// g.yo dang sgyu bral bsam pa dge ldan pa// nga rgyal dregs med snod kyi dam pa
225b5(phal chen): po/ / khro dang 'tshig med khengs shing 'gying ba med// blta na sdug pa khyod mthong legs pa yin// tshur shog phyogs kun spyod yul mngon gyur pa// tshur sho ga rgyal ba'i mdzod rnams sbub byed pa//
225b6(phal chen): tshur shog rgyal ba'i mdzod rnams 'phel byed pa// yid la dub med legs par khyod 'ongs sam// tshur shog dus gsum yul ldan 'ongs pa legs// chos kyi dbyings la mos pa'i dkyil
225b7(phal chen): 'khor ldan/ / sangs rgyas kun gyi yon tan snying por byung // mkhas pa legs par 'ongs sam mingal lam// tshur shog 'jam dpal ye shes pad+mo'i mchog/ tshur shog sprin dpal char
226a1(phal chen): bas rnam spel ba/ / rgyal ba kun gyi sras kyis btang ba tshur// khyod la bsgribs pa med pa'i phyogs kyang bstan// ltos shig smon lam dra ba ci 'dru ga// chos
226a2(phal chen): dbyings rgyas 'gengs bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod la lam bsgrubs pa// rgya che yangs byed nor bzangs 'dir 'ongs so// bde bar gshegs pa'i spyod yul chol byed
226a3(phal chen): cing / / rdul dang bral ba'i spyod pa 'gro ba'i phyir// smon lam rlabs chen yongs su 'dri byed cing // skyob pa'i yid med 'di ni 'dir 'ongs so// 'das pa'i mgon pos gang la bslab mdzad de//
226a4(phal chen): de bzhin ma byon rnams kyang slob 'gyur la// bde gshegs bzhugs pa'i spyod par bya ba rnams// yongs su dri phyir 'di ni 'dir 'ongs so// 'di ni bdag gi dge ba shes chos smra ba// chos kun nan
226a5(phal chen): tan yongs su ston byed pa/ / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod lam yongs ston pa// yin zhes sems gcig bsam nas 'dir 'ongs so// byang chub sems dpa' bdag gi blo skye ba// sangs rgyas sras
226a6(phal chen): po byang chub skye dbyed pa/ / 'di dag bdag bshes sangs rgyas bsngags pa zhes// de ltar dge ba'i sems kyis 'dir 'ongs so// 'di dag skyed pas bdag gi ma lta bu// yon tan 'o ma sdud pasam
226a7(phal chen): ma 'dra/ / byang chub yan lag yongs su myong ba yin// dge bshes 'di dag gnod pa rnam par zlog/ rga shi thar byed sman pa lta bu ste// bdud rtsi char 'bebs brgya byin lha dbang 'dra// zla ba lta
226b1(phal chen): bur dkar po'i phyogs kyis rgyas/ / zhi ba'i phyogs ston nyi ma gsal ba 'dra// dgra dang grogs la ri bo 'dra ba ste// rgya mtsho bzhin du mi 'khrugs sems dang ldan// yongs su skyong dang mnyan
226b2(phal chen): pa 'dra ba zhes/ / de 'dra'i sems kyis nor bzangs 'dir 'ongs so// 'jigs med skyob pas dpa' bo lta bu ste// ded dpon mgon dang skyabs su gyur pa yin// 'di dag bdag la bde
226b3(phal chen): stobs dmigs yin zhes/ / de 'dra'i sems kyis dge ba shes bsnyen bkur byed// chos kyi phyogs rnams rtag tu ston pa ste// sangs rgyas yon tan ye shes ston pa yin// ngan song ngan/
226b4(phal chen): 'gro thams cad sbyor bar byed// dge ba shes 'di dag bdag la dge ba ston// 'di dag rgyal ba'i mdzod kun stobs pa yin// 'di dag rgyal ba kun gyi mdzod srungs te// 'di dag rgyal ba
226b5(phal chen): kun gyi gsang 'dzin ces/ / de ltar mkhas pa 'di ni dge ba shes bsnyen// ye shes 'phun ldan 'di las rnam par dag/ gzugs dang longs spyod tshe rigs phun sum tshogs// 'di las/
226b6(phal chen): phun sum tshogs kun dkon pa min// bsam pa de 'dras 'di ni 'dir 'ongs so// bsam pa rlabs chen 'di la kun kyang ltos// mkhas pa'i dge ba shes rnams la 'di rten cing // mkhas
226b7(phal chen): pa 'di tho ci 'dra skyed pa ltos/ / khyed kyis rtag tu de ltar bslab par bya// 'di ni sngon gyi bsod nams dge ba'i rgyus// byang chubazhugs te 'jam dpal mthong gyur nas// de yi
227a1(phal chen): gdams ngag rjes su mthun spyod cing / / skyo ba med par rgyu ba 'di la spros// 'dis ni dga' bde thams cad kun spangs te// lha rdzas lta bu'i khyim yang yongs
227a2(phal chen): su spangs/ / pa ma ma ma spyod pa rgya chen kun// yongs su spangs shing zan ltar bshes gnyen sten// mkhas pa 'dis ni bsam pa rnam sbyangs te// bdag gis mi lus yongs su spang byas
227a3(phal chen): nas/ / sangs rgyas kun gyi pho brang 'gro bar 'gyur// de phyir 'bras bu de 'dra'ang thob par 'gyur// 'dis ni rgan dang nad kyis mnar ba yi// srog chags sdug bsngal brgya yi sa gtses pa rnams//
227a4(phal chen): skye shi mya ngan 'jigs pas gdungs mthong nas// de dag don du snying rje'i sems kyis spyod// 'gro rgyud lnga yi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor du// sdug bsngal 'khrul 'khor btsir ba'i 'gro mthong
227a5(phal chen): nas/ / sdug bsngal 'khrul 'khor 'khor lo 'jom pa yi// ye shes rdo rje sras pa 'di tshal lo// 'dod chags zhe sdang rtswa sdong tsher ma can// lha chags rtswa mang yongs su 'dzings pa yi//
227a6(phal chen): sems can zhing ni yongs su sbyang ba'i phyir// shes rab ka shol brtan bzang po 'di tshol lo// gti mug ma rig thibs po'i bsam pa can// 'gro ba shes rab mig stor dmigs med
227a7(phal chen): pa/ / de la phyogs bde ston pa'i mthu yod pa// 'gro ba'i ded dpon bzang por 'di 'gyur ro// bzod pa'i gro bgos rnam thar bzhon pa zhon// ye shes ral gris mya ngan dgra 'jom
227b1(phal chen): pas/ / mi 'jigs stobs pa'i dpa' bor gyur pa 'di// 'gro ba rnams kyi lam ston 'gyur ba yin// 'di ni chos kyi gru rab sbyor ba ste// ye shes rgya mtsho'i lam la bslabs

227b3(phal chen): pa'i/ / chos dbyings mkha' la 'od chen rab ldan par// 'di ni khams gsum nyi mar 'char bar 'gyur// byams pa'i dga' ldan ting 'dzin dang bsil ba'i// sems can kun la
227b4(phal chen): snyoms sems 'od bzang la/ / dkar po'i chos kyi dkyil 'khor yongs rgyas pa'i// sangs rgyas zla ba 'di ni 'char bar 'gyur// bsam pa'i gzhi rten brtan la rab gnas pa// byang chub
227b5(phal chen): spyod pas rim gyis 'phags pa ste/ / chos kun rin chen 'byung gnas ldan pa yi// ye shes rgya mtsho'i mchog tu 'di 'gyur ro// byang chub sems kyi klu yi dbang gis phyung // chos kyi
227b6(phal chen): dbyings kyi mkha' la mngon par 'phags/ / dkar po'i 'bras bu'i lo tog 'phel byed pa'i// 'di ni 'gro bar chos sprin char 'bebs 'gyur// dag pa'i snying po dri gsum mun sel ba//
227b7(phal chen): byams pa'i snum yod dran pa'i snod brtan pa// dri med byang chub sems skyed 'od bzang ba'i// chos kyi mar me 'di ni 'bar byed 'gyur// byang chub sems ni mar mer snying rje sko//
228a1(phal chen): byams pa rdos pa mi g.yo bsam pa mkhregs// byang chub yan lag mthar gyis byung ba yi// sangs rgyas sras su 'di ni yang dag skye// bsod nams snying po mngon
228a2(phal chen): par 'phel bar byed/ / ye shes snying po yongs su sbyong bar 'gyur// 'di ni shes pa'i snying po 'char bar byed// smon lam ji bzhin snying po yang dag byung // snying rje byams pas sprul pa 'di
228a3(phal chen): 'drag/ / sems can dgrol blo phan pa'i bsam ldan pa// rnam dag yid can 'di ni ci 'ja ba// de rnga'i 'gro ba lha dang mir bcas dkon// 'di 'dra'i bsam pa rab tu rtsa brtan la// 'di
228a4(phal chen): 'dra'i sbyor ba brtan pas rnam 'phel cing / / srid gsum yog par byed pa 'di 'dra ba'i// ye shes shing chen 'bras bu 'byung ba dkon// 'di ni yon tan kun sgrub don du gnyer// chos rnams
228a5(phal chen): thams cad yongs su dri bar mos/ / the tshom thams cad rnam par bsal don du// le lo med par bshes gnyen thams cad ste// 'di ni bdud kyi dkrugs ma nyon mongs 'jom// 'di ni lta ba'i dri ma srid

249b3(phal chen): ye shes kyi dbyings kyi yul snang bar mdzad pa de srid du lnga dang / ma dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba zag pa yod pa 'am/ zag pa med pa
249b4(phal chen): gang ji snyed pa de dag thams cad kyis kyang byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i nor bu rin po che chen po dbang gi rgyal po'i rin du mi chog go/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na nor bu rin po
249b5(phal chen): che chen po rgya mtsho'i rgyan gyi dam pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de ni rgya mtsho'i rgyan thams cad yongs su ston to// de bzhin du byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i nor bu rin po che chen po rgya
249b6(phal chen): mtsho'i rgyan gyi dam pa'ang thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul rgya mtsho'i rgyan tham cad yongs su ston to/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na nor bu rin po che chen po yid bzhin gyi
249b7(phal chen): rgyal po ma gtogs par lha rdzas kyi 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser las lhag par 'phags pa gang yang med do/ / de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes nor bu rin po che chen po yid bzhin
250a1(phal chen): gyi rgyal po ma gtogs par/ byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i lha rdzas kyi 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser las lhag par khyad par du 'phags pa gang yang med do//
250a2(phal chen): rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na klu'i tshogs grub par gyur pa'i sprul 'dul ba ni klu dang sbrul thams cad la dbang gyur ro// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed
250a3(phal chen): pa'i nan tan gyi klu'i dkyil 'khor grub pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sbrul 'dul ba'ang nyon mongs pa'i klu dang sbrul thams cad la dbang sgyur ro/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na
250a4(phal chen): dpa' bo lag cha dang ldan pa ni dgra'i 'khor gyis tshugs par dka' 'o/ / de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i lag cha dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
250a5(phal chen): thams cad kyang nyon mongs pa'i dgra'i dkyil 'khor thams cad kyis thub par dka' 'o/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na lha rdzas kyi tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i phye ma srang
250a6(phal chen): gcig gis ni stong gsum gyi 'jig rten gyi khams dri zhim pos rgyas par 'geng ste/ de zho gcig tsam la'ang stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rin po ches yongs su gang bas
250a7(phal chen): rin du mi chog go/ / de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa lha rdzas kyi tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po lhag pa'i bsam pa gcig la gnas pa'i khams kyang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad
250b1(phal chen): yon tan gyi dri zhim pos rgyas par 'gengs te/ slob pa dang / mi slob pa dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sems kyang zil gyis gnon to// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na tsan dan rin
250b2(phal chen): po che chen po kha ba'i tsan dan zhes bya ba ni gdung ba thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed de/ lus thams cad kyang rab tu bsil bar byed do// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i kha ba'i
250b3(phal chen): tsan dan rin po che'ang nyon mongs pa'i kun tu rtog pa dang / 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug gi gdung ba thams cad kyang rab tu sel to// ye shes kyi lus kyang rab tu sim par byed do//
250b4(phal chen): rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyi drung du ji snyed cig nye bar 'dod ba de dag thams cad kyang gser gyi kha dog tu kha dog gcig tu 'gyur ro// de bzhin du gang su'ang rung ste/ thams
250b5(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' drung du nye bar 'ongs pa de dag thams cad kyang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi kha dog tu kha dog gcig par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi
250b6(phal chen): bu 'di lta ste/ dper na shing sus kyang mi tshugs pa dang kun nas 'du ba'i shun phrags kyi dri zhim po 'byung ba de lta bu ni/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi me tog bar shi ka dang / me tog dza ti dang / me tog su man la
250b7(phal chen): sogs pa me tog gi rnam pa thams cad la'ang med do/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i sa bon las byung ba'i smon lam gyi shing gi yon tan dang / ye shes kyi shun
251a1(phal chen): thags kyi dri zhim po'i ngad 'byung ba de lta bu ni dge ba'i rtsa ba dma' ba dang ldan pa thams cad dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi me tog par shi ka dang / me tog dza ti dang /
251a2(phal chen): me tog su ma na'i tshul khrims dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / shes rab dang / rnam par grol ba dang / rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba zag pa med pa dang ldan pa thams cad la'ang med do// rigs kyi
251a3(phal chen): bu 'di lta ste/ dper na shing sus kyang mi thub pa dang / kun nas 'du ba kha 'bus par gyur na/ me tog stong phrag mang po'i 'byung gnas su gyur par shes par bya'o// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid
251a4(phal chen): du sems bskyed pa'i shing kun nas 'du ba dge ba'i rtsa bas kha 'bus par gyur na/ lha dang mi grangs med pa'i byang chub kyi me tog zag pa dang bcas pa dang / zag pa med pa'i skye gnas su 'gyur bar shes
251a5(phal chen): par bya'o/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na shing kun nas 'du ba'i me tog gis nyi ma gcig tu bsgos pa'i gos sam/ til mar las dri zhim po'i ngad 'byung ba de lta bu'ang me tog tsam pa ka dang / me tog
251a6(phal chen): su ma nas nyi ma brgya phrag stong du bsgos pa'i gos sam/ til mar las kyang mi 'byung ngo // de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems kyi rgyud tshe gcig tu yongs su bsgos pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i yon
251a7(phal chen): tan dang / ye shes kyi dri zhim po'i ngang phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhabs kyi drung du ldang ba de lta bu ni bskal pa brgya phrag stong du bsgos pa'i nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sems las kyang zag pa med pa'i
251b1(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba dang chos kyi ye shes kyi dri zhim po mi 'byung ngo / / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na shing gi rigs na li kai re zhes bya ba rgya mtsho gnod pa dang bral ba nas skye ba yod do// de'i rtsa ba yan chad me tog gi
251b2(phal chen): bar du'ang dus thams cad du nam du'ang sems can rnams kyi nye bar 'tsho bar mi 'gyur ba med do/ / de bzhin du snying rje chen po dang smon lam gyi rtsa ba yang dag par skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yang thog ma
251b3(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa nas nye bar bzung ba phyin chad dam pa'i chos gnas pa'i mthar thug gi bar du nam yang lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi nye bar 'tsho bar mi 'gyur ba med do/ / rigs kyi
251b4(phal chen): bu 'di lta ste/ dper na dngul chu'i rigs gser du snang ba zhes bya ba yod do// de ni srang gcig gis kyang lcags srang stong gser du 'gyur ro// dngul chu srang gcig pu de ni lcags srang stong po des zad par bya ba
251b5(phal chen): 'am/ lcags su bsgyur bar mi nus so// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i ro'i khams dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bsngos pa'i ye shes kyis bzung ba ni las dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib
251b6(phal chen): pa'i lcags thams cad zad par byas te/ chos thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi kha dog tu byed kyang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i ro'i khams gcig pu de ni/ las dang nyon mongs
251b7(phal chen): pa'i lcags thams cad kyis kyang kun nas nyon mongs par bya ba 'am/ zad par mi nus so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na me ni ji tsam du chung ngu zin kyang rkyen ji tsam dang phrad pa de tsam gyi se lce yongs su skyed do/
252a1(phal chen): de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i me ji tsam du chung ngu zin kyang dmigs pa rgya chen po'i tshogs kyi rkyen ji tsam dang phrad pa de tsam du ye shes kyi 'od 'phro ba rab
252a2(phal chen): tu dgye bas rnam par 'phel bar byed do/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na me mar gcig las me mar bye ba brgya phrag stong zhig bus kyang / me mar de ni de snyed byung bas mi zad de mthar thug pa med do// de bzhin
252a3(phal chen): du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i me mar gcig las 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du thugs bskyed pa'i
252a4(phal chen): me mar mang po 'bar yang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i me mar gcig pu de ni de snyed kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i me mar byung bas mi zad de mthar thug pa med do/ /
252a5(phal chen): rigs bu 'di lta ste/ dper na me mar gcig cig khyim mam khang bu ji lta bur bcug kyang rung ste/ bcug ma thag tu lo stong du bsags pa'i mun pa'ang rnam par sel cing snang bar byed do//
252a6(phal chen): de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems bskyed pa gcig kyang sems can gyi bsam pa'i khyim thibs po ma rig pa'i mun pa dang ldan pa ji lta bu'ang rung ste/ de'i rgyud du phyin na de phyin ma thag tu
252a7(phal chen): bskal pa brgya stong brjod du med par bsags pa'i las dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / mun pa thams cad rnam par sel cing ye shes kyi snang ba yongs su skyed do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper
252b1(phal chen): na me mar ni snying po ji tsam pa de'i rkyen tsam du snang bar byed de/ mar gyi tshogs ji srid du gnas pa de srid du 'bar ro// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i ma mar yang / byang
252b2(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i smon lam gyi snying po'i khyad par ci 'dra ba de lta bur chos kyi dbyings yongs su snang bar byed de/ snying rje chen pos spyod pa'i mar gyi tshogs ji srid du gnas pa de srid du/ sems can gdul
252b3(phal chen): ba dang / zhing yongs su dag par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku don bsgrub pa la yongs su 'bar bar gnas so// // shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas phal po che
252b4(phal chen): zhes bya ba las sdong pos brgyan pa'i le'u ste/ bam po brgya bcu gsum pa/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na lha rdzas kyi 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi rgyan lha'i rgyal po dbar sgyur
252b5(phal chen): gyi mgo la thogs pa ni/ 'dod pa la spyod pa'i lha'i bu thams cad kyis ma 'phrogs so// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa lha rdzas kyi 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi rgyan nan
252b6(phal chen): tan dang / yon tan la rab tu gnas pa byang chub sems dpa' phyir mi ldog pa rnams kyi smon lam chen po'i mgo la thogs pa ni/ byis pa tha dad pa'i skye bo dang / slob pa dang / mi slob pa dang / rang
252b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyis mi 'phrogs so/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na ri dwags kyi rgyal po seng ge'i nga ros ni seng ge'i phrug gu skyes nas ring po ma lon pa'ang nyams su bde zhing rnga'i/ ri dgas thams
253a1(phal chen): cad ni kun tu 'byer bar 'gyur ro/ / de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa skyes bu'i seng ge chen po'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi nga ro byang chub kyi sems yongs su rjod pa phyung bas ni
253a2(phal chen): las dang po pa'i byang chub sems dpa' seng ge'i phrug gu rnams sangs rgyas kyi chos kyis nyams su bde zhing rta'i/ dmigs pa la gnas pa'i sems can thams cad ni kun tu 'byer ro// rigs kyi bu 'di
253a3(phal chen): lta ste/ dper na seng ge'i rgyus pa las rgyud du byas pa'i pi wang gi sgras ni pi wang thams cad kyi rgyud yongs su 'chad do// de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i sku mnga' ba'i byed
253a4(phal chen): chub tu sems bskyed pa'i rgyus pa'i yon tan brjod pa'i sgras 'dod pa'i rgyud kyi dga' ba'i pi wang thams cad kyi rgyud yongs su 'chad par 'gyur ro/ / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa dang
253a5(phal chen): yon tan gyi gtam thams cad kyang yongs su 'gag par 'gyur ro/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na rgya mtsho chen po ba dang / ma he dang / ra'i 'o mas yongs su gang ba'i nang du seng ge'i 'o ma
253a6(phal chen): thigs gcig blugs pas/ 'o ma thams cad 'gyes par 'gyur te 'dur mi btub bo// de bzhin du bskal pa brgya phrag stong du bsags pa'i nyon mongs pa kun gyi 'o ma'i rgya mtshor yang de bzhin
253a7(phal chen): gshegs pa skyes bu'i seng ge chen po'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i 'o ma'i thigs pa gcig blugs pas thams cad ma lus par zad par 'gyur te/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas
253b1(phal chen): thams cad kyi rnam par thar pa rnams kyang mi gnas mi 'du'o/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na bya ka la bing ka'i phrug gu sgo nga'i sbubs nas ma byung ba la nga ro'i mthu'i khyad par yod pa de lta bu ni/
253b2(phal chen): gangs kyi ri la gnas pa'i bya'i tshogs mthu dang shugs thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa thams cad la'ang med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' ka la bing ka'i phrug gu las dang po pa 'khor
253b3(phal chen): ba'i sgo ba'i sbubs na 'dug pa la snying rje chen po dang / byang chub kyi sems kying ro'i mthu'i khyad par yod pa de lta bu ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad la med do// rigs kyis
253b4(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha' lding chen po'i phrug gu skyes nas ring po ma lon pa la gshog pa'i rlung gi stobs dang / mthu bdog pa dang / mig yongs su dag pa'i yon tan yod pa de lta/
253b5(phal chen): bu ni/ de ma yin pa'i bya lus tshad du phyin pa gzhan thams cad la'ang med do// de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa nam mkha' lding chen po'i rigs dang / rgyad du byung ba'i byang chub sems
253b6(phal chen): dpa' nam mkha' lding chen po'i phrug gu sems dang po bskyed pa la thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i gshog pa'i rlung gi stobs dang / shugs bdog pa dang / snying rje chen po dang /
253b7(phal chen): lhag pa'i bsam pa'i mig yongs su dag pa'i yon tan yod pa'i nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas bskal pa brgya stong tshang bas byung ba thams cad la med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na skyes bu chen po'i lag
254a1(phal chen): nas spyad pa'i mde'u thung gis ni go cha ji tsam du sra'ang brtol to/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus brtan pa dang ldan pa'i lag nas spyad pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa
254a2(phal chen): nyid du sems bskyed pa'i mde'u thung gis kyang lta ba dang bag la nyal ba'i go cha thams cad mi brtol ba med do/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na mthu bo che chen po khros te brngam pa'i dpral ba la thor
254a3(phal chen): bu ji srid du gnas pa de srid du 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi thams cad kyis kyang mi thub bo/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' mthu bo che chen po snying rje chen po badras pa'i lhan pa'i bsam pa'i gdong la thams cad mkhyen
254a4(phal chen): pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i thor bu ji srid du gnas pa de srid du/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gtogs pa'i bdud thams cad dang / bdud kyi las thams cad kyis kyang mi thub bo// rigs kyi bu
254a5(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ dper na 'phong gi slob dpon gyi mtshan bu ma byang ba 'phong gi thabs la ma goms pa la 'phong gi gnas dang / thabs kyi mthu dang / khyad par bdog pa de lta bu ni thams cad la byang
254a6(phal chen): yang 'bong mi shes pa rnams la med do/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' cang shes las dang po pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sa la goms pa la smon lam gyi ye shes dang mos pas spyod pa'i mthu'i
254a7(phal chen): khyad par ci bdog pa de lta bu ni/ byang chub tu sems ma bskyed pa'i sems can thams cad dang / slob pa dang / mi slob pa dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad la med do// rigs kyi bu
254b1(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ dper na 'phong slob pa'i 'phong gi rgyus thams cad la ni dang por rkang pa'i stangs la goms par bya ba la sngon du 'gro'o// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid
254b2(phal chen): kyi sa la slob pas sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad khong du chud par bya ba la'ang / dang por thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa la yang dag par gnas pa sngon du 'gro'o//
254b3(phal chen): rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na sgyu ma'i mkhan po sgyu ma'i rnam pa dang / yul thams cad yongs su ston pa'i bya ba thams cad ni dang por sngags kyi dngos grub mngon par bsgrub pa yid la byas na
254b4(phal chen): 'grub par 'gyur ro/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i yul dang / rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su ston pa'i sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yul thams cad la'ang
254b5(phal chen): dang po sems bskyed pa'i smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa ni yongs su grub pa yin no/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na sgyu ma'i sngags dang / rig sngags thams cad ni gzugs med la bstan
254b6(phal chen): du med pa yin yang / sems bskyed pas sgyu ma'i sprul pa dang / gzugs kyi rnam pa thams cad yongs su ston to// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'ang gzugs
254b7(phal chen): med la/ bstan du med de/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad sems bskyed pa la dbang sgyur ba tsam gyis chos kyi dbyings thams cad yon tan gyi rgyan rnam par phye ba thams cad kyis rnam par sgrub bo// rigs
255a1(phal chen): kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na byi la'i mig gis blta ba tsam gyis byi ba thams cad kun tu 'byor ro// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems
255a2(phal chen): bskyed pa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa'i sbyor ba tsam gyis las dang nyon mongs pa thams cad 'byer bar 'gyur ro/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi rgyan btags na rgyan thams
255a3(phal chen): cad zil gyis gnon to/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' byang chub kyi sems 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi rgyan thogs pa'ang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yon tan gyi rgyan zil
255a4(phal chen): gyis gnon to/ / zil du rlag par byed do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na rdzob khab long gi rgyal po'i khams ji tsam du chung yang lcags sgrog sra ba thams cad zhigs par byed do//
255a5(phal chen): de bzhin du sems thag pa nas bskyed pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i khams ji tsam du chung yang lta ba'i rnam pa dang / ma rig pa dang / sred pa'i sgrog thams cad zhigs
255a6(phal chen): par byed do/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na rdo ba khab long gi khams ni gang dang gang du bzhag pa de dang der lcags phal pa thams cad 'gyes shing mi gnas la mi 'du'o// de bzhin du
255a7(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i khams kyang las sam/ nyon mongs pa 'am/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi rnam grol ba gang dang gang du byung ba de dang de dag gi las dang /
255b1(phal chen): nyon mongs pa thams cad dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa thams cad kyang 'byer zhing mi 'khod mi 'du'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na chu srin gyi tshil gyi zags
255b2(phal chen): ma gcig zos pa'i nye pa ni chu'i srog chags thams cad kyi 'jigs pa dang bral ba yin te/ chu srin gyis sos btab kyang lus la mi tshugs so// de bzhin du lhag pa'i bsam pas byang chub kyi
255b3(phal chen): sems kyi cha gcig zos pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yang 'khor ba'i las dang / nyon mongs pa'i 'jigs pa dang bral ba yin te/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis mngon par
255b4(phal chen): khong du chud par bya ba'i nang na 'dug kyang yang dag pa'i mtha' mngon du bya ba'i lam gol bar ltung bas gnod par mi 'gyur ro/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na bdud rtsi'i chu 'thungs pa'i skyes bu ni
255b5(phal chen): gzhan gyis gnod par bya ba thams cad kyis mi 'chi'o/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i bdud rtsi'i chu 'thungs pa'ang / nyan thos dang rang sangs
255b6(phal chen): rgyas thams cad kyi sar mi 'chi'o/ / byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po'i smon lam las kyang rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na bsku bsgrub pa'i skyes bu ni mi'i gnas
255b7(phal chen): thams cad rnam par spyod kyang mi kun gyis mi mthong ngo / / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i shes rab dang / smon lam gyis nye bar brtan pa bdud kyi yul thams cad la rnam
256a1(phal chen): par spyod kyang bdud thams cad kyis mi mthong ngo / / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na rgyal po chen po la rten pa'i skyes bu ni skye bo ma rabs thams cad kyis mi 'jigs so//
256a2(phal chen): de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa chos kyi rgyal po chen po la rten pa'ang / sgrib pa dang / bar chad dang / ngan song thams cad kyis mi 'jigs so//
256a3(phal chen): rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na sa phug gi khyim na gnas na/ sa'i gseb thams cad rlan gyis yongs su gang bas me'i 'jigs pa med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems kyi rgyud byang chub kyi
256a4(phal chen): sems kyi dge ba'i rtsa bas mngon par brlan pa la'ang / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi rnam par grol ba'i ye shes kyi mes 'jigs pa med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na dpa' bo
256a5(phal chen): la rten pa'i mi ni dgra thams cad kyis mi 'jigs so/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa dpa' bo la rten pa'ang spyod pa ngan pa'i dgra thams cad
256a6(phal chen): kyis mi 'jigs so/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na lha'i dbang po brgya byin rdo rje'i lag cha thogs pa ni/ lha ma yin gyi tshogs thams cad rab tu 'jom mo// de bzhin du byang chub sems
256a7(phal chen): dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa brtan pa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa rdo rje'i lag cha thogs pa'ang bdud dang phas kyi rgol ba'i lha ma yin gyi tshogs thams cad rab tu 'jom mo/ /
256b1(phal chen): rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na rtsi ro'i bcud 'thungs pa'i skyes bu ni tshe shin tu ring bar gnas so// nyam chung bar mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad
256b2(phal chen): mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i ro'i bcud kyi tshogs 'thungs pa'ang bskal pa grangs med par 'khor yang yongs su skyo ba med la 'khor ba'i skyon gyis mi gos so/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/
256b3(phal chen): dper na sman gyi ro sbyar ro cog thams cad du chu ni sngon du 'gro ba ste/ gang la'ang skyon du mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin du byang chu sems dpa'i spyod pa dang smon lam gyi tshogs sbyar ba thams cad du
256b4(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa ni sngon du 'gro ste/ gang la skyon du mi 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na mi'i don du bya ba thams cad la ni srog gi dbang po sngon du
256b5(phal chen): 'gro'o/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpas sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par blang ba la'ang byang chub kyi sems sngon du 'gro'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na skyes bu srog gi
256b6(phal chen): dbang po dang bral ba ni las thams cad la mthu med pas pha ma dang / gnyen bshes kyi tshogs kyis kyang nye bar 'tsho bar byar med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa
256b7(phal chen): nyid du sems bskyed pa dang bral ba'ang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes thob par bya ba la mthu med pas/ sems can thams cad kyis kyang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi yon tan gyis nye bar 'tsho bar byar

257a2(phal chen): chen po'ang las dang / nyon mongs pa dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas su sems bskyed pa'i dug thams cad kyis gdug par mi nus so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na nyi ma'i dkyil
257a3(phal chen): 'khor ni skar ma thams cad kyi 'od kyis thub par mi nus so/ / de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor yang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi skar ma thams cad
257a4(phal chen): kyi yon tan zag pa med pa'i 'od kyis mi thub bo/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na rgyal po'i bu skyes nas yun ring du ma lon pa'ang / blon po'i mchog tu bya ba nas rgan pa thams cad rigs su
257a5(phal chen): rigs dang ldan par skyes pa dang dbang gse zil gyis gnon to/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' byang chub tu sems bskyed nas ring po ma lon pa/ chos kyi rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs
257a6(phal chen): su skyes pa'i las dang po pa'ang / yun ring po nas tshangs par spyod spyod pa'i nyan thos nas rgan pa thams cad byang chub kyi sems kyi snying rje chen po'i dbang gis zil gyis gnon to// rigs kyi bu 'di
257a7(phal chen): lta ste/ dper na blon po ji tsam du nas rgan pas kyang rgyal bu gzhon nu ji tsam du chung ba la'ang phyag bya dgos so// rgyal po'i bus kyang blon po rgan po la rim gro mi bya ba ma yin no// de bzhin du
257b1(phal chen): nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas ji tsam du rgan la/ ji tsam du tshangs pa'i spyod pa ring du spyod spyod pa rnams kyis kyang / byang chub sems dpa' las dang po pa la gdud par bya'o// byang chub sems
257b2(phal chen): dpas kyang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas rnams la rim gro med par bya ba ma yin no/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na rgyal po'i bu thams cad kyis mi dgos par bya ba zhig na'ang rgyal po'i
257b3(phal chen): mtshan dang ldan na/ rigs kyis btsun pas rgyal po'i blon po dam par bya ba thams cad dang yang mi mnyam mo// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' las dang nyon mongs pa'i nye bar len pa
257b4(phal chen): thams cad kyis non pa'ang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i mtshan dang ldan na/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs kyis btsun zhing che bas nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas mchog tu phyin pa thams cad
257b5(phal chen): dang yang mi mnyam mo/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na nor bu rin po che yongs su dag pa ni mig la rab ribi kyi skyon yod na yongs su ma dag par snang ngo // de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen
257b6(phal chen): pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rin po che rang bzhin gyis yongs su dag pa'ang sems can dad pa'i mig mi shes pa'i rab rib kyi skyon dang ldan pa rnams la yongs su ma dag par snang ngo / / rigs kyi bu 'di lta
257b7(phal chen): / dper na rtsi'i gzungs sngags dang rtsi thams cad bsdus te byas pa ni rig gam/ mthong ngam/ 'grogs na'ang sems can gyi nang rab tu zhi bar byed do// de bzhin du byang chub kyi sems
258a1(phal chen): kyi sems kyi smon lam dang / ye shes kyi lus dge ba'i rtsa ba'i tshogs dang / shes rab dang / thabs kyi sngags dang / rtsi thams cad las bsgrubs pa byang chub kyi sems
258a2(phal chen): dang ldan pa ni thos sam/ mthong ngam/ 'grogs sam/ rjes su dran pa'i tshul gyis kyang sems can gyi nyon mongs pa'i nad rab tu zhi bar byed do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper
258a3(phal chen): na gos dang ba'i mtshan nyid can ni 'idam gyi nyes pa thams cad kyis mi gos so/ / de bzhin du byang chub kyi sems kyi gos dang ba'i mtshan nyid can ni 'khor ba'i nyon mongs pa 'dam gyi skyon thams cad
258a4(phal chen): kyis kun nas nyon mongs par mi 'gyur ro/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na shing gi gzugs mgo gzer gyis btab pa ni yongs su 'gyes par mi 'gyur te bya ba thams cad kyang byed do//
258a5(phal chen): de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du smon pa'i ye shes kyis lus kyi spyi bo byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i smon lam gyi gzer gyis btab pa'ang byang chub sems dpa'i bya ba thams cad la mthu
258a6(phal chen): yod do/ / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi smon lam gyi ye shes las lus su grub pa yin pas yongs su 'gyes par mi 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na gzer dang mi ldan
258a7(phal chen): pa'i 'khrul 'khor ni shing gi yan lag de nyid yin yang dgos pa bya ba'i mthu med do/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa
258b1(phal chen): dang mi ldan na/ byang chub kyi yan lag gi tshogs de nyid yin yang / sangs rgyas kyi chos bsgrub pa la mthu med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po la
258b2(phal chen): r in po che a ka ru nag po glang po'i snying po zhes bya ba yod pa des bdugs ma thag tu rgyal po 'khor los sgyur ba'i yan lag bzhi pa'i dpung gi tshogs thams cad kyang nam mkha' la gnas par
258b3(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ / de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa a ka rus bdugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyang khams gsum pa thams cad las rnam
258b4(phal chen): par 'das te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes nam mkha'i spyod yul 'dus ma byas pa thams cad kyi mthar thug par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na rdo rje ni rin po che ma rabs
258b5(phal chen): kyi 'byung khung nas mi 'byung gi/ rdo rje'i 'byung khung ngam/ gser gyi 'byung khung nas 'byung ngo // de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rdo rje lta bu'ang sems can gyi bsam pa'i
258b6(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba ma rabs kyi rin po che'i 'byung gnas nas mi skye ste/ gzhan du na sems can yongs su skyob pa'i snying rje chen po'i rdo rje'i 'byung khung ngam/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la lhag
258b7(phal chen): par dmigs pa'i gser gyi 'byung khung chen po nas 'byung ngo / / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na shing gi rigs rtsa ba med pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de'i rtsa ba mthar thug pa mi dmigs mod kyi shing
259a1(phal chen): rnams la yal ga dang / lo ma dang / 'dab ma dang / me tog shin tu rgyas pa dra ba lta bur gyur pa snang ngo // de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed
259a2(phal chen): pa'i rtsa ba'i mthar thug pa'ang mi dmigs mod kyi/ 'jig rten gyi skyed gnas thams cad du'ang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bsod nams dang / ye shes dang / mngon par shes pa'i
259a3(phal chen): me tog shin tu rgyas pa smon lam chen po'i dri bar gyur pa'ang yongs su snang ngo / / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na rdo rje ni snod ngan pa'i gzhi la 'dug na mdzes par mi snang ngo // snod ma brdol
259a4(phal chen): ba ma gtogs par snod rdol ba dang bu ga can gyis gzung bar mi nus so/ / de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i rdo rje chen po'ang sems can mos pa zhan pa'i snod dang / ser
259a5(phal chen): sna can nam/ tshul khrims ngan pa can nam/ gnod sems can nam/ le lo can nam/ dran pa 'khrugs pa 'am/ shes rab 'chal pa'i rnams la mi mdzes te/ byang chub

261a1(phal chen): mi 'gyur ro/ / de bzhin du byang chub tu sems bskyed pa rdo rje sra ba'i gzhi la rten pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam rnams kyang khams gsum thams cad du 'jig par mi

262a6(phal chen): gyur to/ / des mthong ba khang pa brtsegs pa de shin tu rgya che zhing yangs la/ rgyar dpag tshad brgya stong mang po dang ldan pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi tshad kyis gzhal ba/ 'khor thams cad du nam

283a3(phal chen): so/ / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad ni phu nu po'o// byang chub kyi sems ni rigs so// nan tan ni rigs kyi chos so// sa'i gnas ni rigs kyi gnas so// bzod pa thob
283a4(phal chen): pa ni rigs su rigs dang ldan par skyes pa'o/ / smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa ni rigs kyi gzhung thob pa'o// spyod pa rnam par dag pa ni rigs kyi chos kyi rjes snyegs pa'o//

283b6(phal chen): kun nas nyon mongs par mi 'gyur ro/ / chos thams cad bdag med par khong du chud pas/ sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul bas yongs su mi skyo'o//
